9-64th Decklists
================



 Posted in **Event Coverage**
 on December 4, 2016 






![](https://media.magic.wizards.com/styles/auth_small/public/images/person/halliesanto_icon.jpg)
By Hallie Santo











Grand Prix Denver demonstrated that there are more than two ways to play Standard. W/U Flash and B/G Delirium decks abounded at the top tables, but we saw plenty of Aetherworks Marvel decks going off with Emrakul and plenty of other combo players doing their thing. If you're at a loss for what to play at your next Friday Night *Magic* or Standard Showdown, look no further than these diverse decklists.







#### Corey Burkhart's R/G Aetherworks – GP Denver, 9th Place


##### 






![](https://web.archive.org/web/20160726232508im_/http://magic.wizards.com/sites/all/modules/features/wiz_bean_content_deck_list/icons/decklist_download.png)
